  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d99d6fa3-708f-4762-a94f-5e6895a39d8d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

              <span id="reviewTextContainer23503282" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15106272538821180497">Falling Up, Shel Silverstein<br/><br/><b>Falling Up</b> is a 1996 poetry collection for children by <b>Shel Silverstein</b>. <br/><br/>It features illustrations, drawn by the author, for most of the 144 poems. Silverstein dedicated the book to his son, <b>Matthew</b>. <br/><br/>It is also the third and final poetry collection by Silverstein in his lifetime, as he died 3 years after Falling Up was released. <br/><br/>Falling Up<br/><br/><i>I tripped on my shoelace<br/>And I fell up -<br/>Up to the rooftops,<br/>Up over the town,<br/>Up past the tree tops,<br/>Up over the mountains,<br/>Up where the</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15106272538821180497" style="display:none">Falling Up, Shel Silverstein<br /><br /><b>Falling Up</b> is a 1996 poetry collection for children by <b>Shel Silverstein</b>. <br /><br />It features illustrations, drawn by the author, for most of the 144 poems. Silverstein dedicated the book to his son, <b>Matthew</b>. <br /><br />It is also the third and final poetry collection by Silverstein in his lifetime, as he died 3 years after Falling Up was released. <br /><br />Falling Up<br /><br /><i>I tripped on my shoelace<br />And I fell up -<br />Up to the rooftops,<br />Up over the town,<br />Up past the tree tops,<br />Up over the mountains,<br />Up where the colors<br />Blend into the sounds.<br />But it got me so dizzy<br />When I looked around,<br />I got sick to my stomach<br />And I threw down.</i><br /><br />عنوانها: سقوط به بالا، بالا افتادن؛ نویسنده: شل سیلور استاین؛ تاریخ نخستین خوانش ماه مارس سال 1997 میلادی، خوانش این نسخه روز نوزدهم ماه آوریل سال 2006 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: بالا افتادن؛ نویسنده: شل سیلور اشتاین؛ مترجم حمید خادمی؛ تهران، پنجره، 1381، در 187 ص؛ چاپ سیزدهم ؛392: شابک 9789649225708؛ موضوع شعر طنز کودکان و نوجوانان از شاعران امریکایی - سده 20 م<br /><br />عنوان: سقوط به بالا: مترجم: رضی خدادای؛ تهران، هوای تازه، 1383؛ در 202 ص؛ شابک 9647222947؛ چاپ سوم تهران، هستان، 1388، در 202 ص؛ شابک 9646965776؛ چاپ چهارم تهران، هستان، شولا، 1394؛ <br /><br />بند کفشم به پایم گیر کرد<br />سکندری خوردم و افتادم بالا<br />بالای پشت بامها<br />بالای درختها<br />بالای کوهها، بالای آنجا که رنگها و صداها باهم یکی میشوند.؛<br />اما وقتی به دور و برم نگاه کردم،؛<br />سرم گیج رفت،؛<br />حال تهوع بهم دست داد<br />و آوردم پایین.؛<br /><b>شل سیلور اشتاین</b><br /><br />برگزین: ا. شربیانی</span>

<div id="review_384141182" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/384141182" />
    <a title="Chin Hwa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4086434-chin-hwa"><img alt="Chin Hwa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1314017149p2/4086434.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/384141182?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chin Hwa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chin Hwa" href="/user/show/4086434-chin-hwa">Chin Hwa</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer384141182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16432995027971782037">Some wonderful gems from this anthology of poems and drawings:<br/><br/>FALLING UP<br/><br/>I tripped on my shoelace<br/>And I fell up--<br/>Up to the roof tops,<br/>Up over the town,<br/>Up past the tree tops,<br/>Up over the mountains,<br/>Up where the colors<br/>Blend into the sounds. <br/>But it got me so dizzy<br/>When I looked around,<br/>I got sick to my stomach<br/>And I threw down.<br/><br/>WOULDA-COULDA-SHOULDA<br/><br/>All the Woulda-Coulda-Shouldas<br/>Layin' in the sun,<br/>Talkin' 'bout the things<br/>They woulda-coulda-shoulda done...<br/>But those Woulda-Coulda-Shouldas<br/>All ran away and hid<br/>Fro</span>
  <span id="freeText16432995027971782037" style="display:none">Some wonderful gems from this anthology of poems and drawings:<br /><br />FALLING UP<br /><br />I tripped on my shoelace<br />And I fell up--<br />Up to the roof tops,<br />Up over the town,<br />Up past the tree tops,<br />Up over the mountains,<br />Up where the colors<br />Blend into the sounds. <br />But it got me so dizzy<br />When I looked around,<br />I got sick to my stomach<br />And I threw down.<br /><br />WOULDA-COULDA-SHOULDA<br /><br />All the Woulda-Coulda-Shouldas<br />Layin' in the sun,<br />Talkin' 'bout the things<br />They woulda-coulda-shoulda done...<br />But those Woulda-Coulda-Shouldas<br />All ran away and hid<br />From one little did.<br /><br />SHARING<br /><br />I'll share your toys, I'll share your money,<br />I'll share your toast, I'll share your honey,<br />I'll share your milk and your cookies too --<br />The hard part's sharing mine with you.<br /><br />KEEP-OUT HOUSE<br /><br />At last--I finished my keep-out house,<br />A house that's meant for privacy,<br />A house that's meant for peacefulness,<br />A house just meant for only me.<br />There is no door where strangers knock,<br />No window where they peek and grin.<br />A perfect private keep-out house...<br />Now...how do I get in?<br /><br />THREE STINGS<br /><br />George got stung by a bee and said,<br />"I wouldn't have got stung if I'd stayed in bed."<br />Fred got stung and we heard him roar,<br />"What am I being punished for?"<br />Lew got stung and we heard him say,<br />"I learned somethin' about bees today."<br /><br />HELP!<br /><br />I walked through the wildwood, and what did I see<br />But a unicorn with his horn stuck in a tree,<br />Cryin', "Someone please help me before it's too late."<br />I hollered, "I'll free you." He hollered back, "Wait--<br />How much will it hurt? How long will it take?<br />Are you sure that my horn will not scratch, bend, or break?<br />How hard will you pull? How much must I pay?<br />Must you do it right now or is Wednesday okay?<br />Have you done this before? Do you have the right tools?<br />Have you graduated from horn-savin' school?<br />Will I owe you a favor? And what will it be?<br />Do you promise that you will not damage the tree?<br />Should I close my eyes? Should I sit down or stand? <br />Do you have insurance? Have you washed your hands?<br />And after you free me--tell me what then?<br />Can you guarantee I won't get stuck again?<br />Tell me when. Tell me how.<br />Tell me why. Tell me where...."<br /><br />I guess that he's still sitting' there.</span>

<div id="review_1850710108" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Michael Finocchiaro" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48483884-michael-finocchiaro"><img alt="Michael Finocchiaro" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576692048p2/48483884.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michael Finocchiaro" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michael Finocchiaro" href="/user/show/48483884-michael-finocchiaro">Michael Finocchiaro</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48483884-michael-finocchiaro?shelf=poetry">poetry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48483884-michael-finocchiaro?shelf=kids">kids</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1850710108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2550165592491448368">As always, a wonderful book of beautiful, funny and endearing poems from Shel Silverstein. My favorites:<br/><br/>Diving Board<br/><br/>You've been up on that diving board<br/>Making sure that it's nice and straight.<br/>You've made sure that it's not too slick.<br/>You've made sure that it can stand the weight.<br/>You've made sure that the spring is tight.<br/>You've made sure that the cloth won't slip.<br/>You've made sure that it bounces right.<br/>And now that your toes can get a grip -<br/>And you've been up there since half past five<br/>Doin everythin</span>
  <span id="freeText2550165592491448368" style="display:none">As always, a wonderful book of beautiful, funny and endearing poems from Shel Silverstein. My favorites:<br /><br />Diving Board<br /><br />You've been up on that diving board<br />Making sure that it's nice and straight.<br />You've made sure that it's not too slick.<br />You've made sure that it can stand the weight.<br />You've made sure that the spring is tight.<br />You've made sure that the cloth won't slip.<br />You've made sure that it bounces right.<br />And now that your toes can get a grip -<br />And you've been up there since half past five<br />Doin everything...but DIVE.<br /><br />And the title poem:<br /><br />Falling Up<br /><br />I tripped on my shoelace<br />And I fell up -<br />Up to the rooftops,<br />Up over the town,<br />Up past the tree tops,<br />Up over the mountains,<br />Up where the colors<br />Blend into the sounds.<br />But it got me so dizzy<br />When I looked around,<br />I got sick to my stomach<br />And I threw down.<br /><br />I am not sure if anyone writes children's poetry quite like Silverstein but it is one of my favorites for sure!</span>

<div id="review_99494388" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/99494388" />
    <a title="Ronyell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell"><img alt="Ronyell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506581787p2/1169488.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/99494388?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronyell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronyell" href="/user/show/1169488-ronyell">Ronyell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Shel Silverstein fans!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=bedtime-stories">bedtime-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=ronyell-s-epinions-reviews">ronyell-s-epinions-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=short-story-collection">short-story-collection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=my-blog-reviews">my-blog-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=children-s-book">children-s-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=gross-humor">gross-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1169488-ronyell?shelf=shel-silverstein">shel-silverstein</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer99494388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1888385206740052084"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334211i/693654.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='Falling Up' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ever since I was little, I have been a huge fan of Shel Silverstein’s works as they were creative, controversial and hilarious to read through! I have practically read almost all of Shel Silverstein’s works including <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30119.Where_the_Sidewalk_Ends' title='Where the Sidewalk Ends by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>Where the Sidewalk Ends</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30118.A_Light_in_the_Attic' title='A Light in the Attic by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Light in the Attic</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10659536.Every_Thing_on_It' title='Every Thing on It by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>Every Thing on It</a> and I had enjoyed every single one of them! Now, I have finally read another one of Shel Silverstein’s books called “Falling Up” and it was just as enjoyable as Shel Silverstein’s other works!<br/><br/>This is another book t</span>
  <span id="freeText1888385206740052084" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334211i/693654.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="Falling Up" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ever since I was little, I have been a huge fan of Shel Silverstein’s works as they were creative, controversial and hilarious to read through! I have practically read almost all of Shel Silverstein’s works including <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30119.Where_the_Sidewalk_Ends" title="Where the Sidewalk Ends by Shel Silverstein" rel="nofollow noopener">Where the Sidewalk Ends</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30118.A_Light_in_the_Attic" title="A Light in the Attic by Shel Silverstein" rel="nofollow noopener">A Light in the Attic</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10659536.Every_Thing_on_It" title="Every Thing on It by Shel Silverstein" rel="nofollow noopener">Every Thing on It</a> and I had enjoyed every single one of them! Now, I have finally read another one of Shel Silverstein’s books called “Falling Up” and it was just as enjoyable as Shel Silverstein’s other works!<br><br>This is another book that has a set of Shel Silverstein’s famous poems and some of the poems featured in this book include:<br><br><b>
  <u>FALLING UP</u>
</b><br><br><i>I tripped on my shoelace<br>And I fell up-<br>Up to the roof tops,<br>Up over the town,<br>Up past the tree tops,<br>Up over the mountains, <br>Up where the colors<br>Blend into the sounds.<br>But it got me so dizzy<br>When I looked around,<br>I got sick to my stomach<br>And I threw down.</i><br><br>Once again, Shel Silverstein had piqued my interest in his talent for writing surreal and hilarious poetry that interest children as well as adults! I loved the wacky style that Shel Silverstein puts into the poems as the characters are always doing bizarre things such as in the poem “Complainin’ Jack” where a Jack-in-a-box just complains all day and in the poem “Rotten Convention” where there is a vast array of horrible characters such as Hamburger Face and Gruesome Grace attending a convention. I also loved Shel Silverstein’s artwork as it is mostly in black and white colorings and is truly surreal to look at. Probably my favorite illustrations in this book was of the image of the pet lion in the poem “Unfair” as it looked incredibly creepy and surreal at the same time and the characters from the poem “Rotten Convention” as they look truly frightening and surreal, especially the image of a man who has a knife going through his head.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334211i/693655.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="Falling Up" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Parents should know that like most of Shel Silverstein’s books, there are some poems that might either frighten children or cause them to perform the crazy stunts that the characters did in this book. Probably some of the most suggestive poems in this book would be “Crazy Dream” which involves a child having a dream about torturing his teachers and that might convince small children to do the same and “Spoiled Brat” where a child is eaten alive which would frighten small children. Parents should probably read this book before they show it to their children to see if they can handle the content in this book.<br><br>Overall, “Falling Up” is a truly brilliant book that contains some of Shel Silverstein’s most memorable poems and many adults and children will definitely enjoy the wacky humor of these poems! I would highly recommend this book to children ages six and up since there are some suggestive content in this book that adults might want to discuss with their children about.<br><br><b>Review is also on: <a href="http://rabbitearsbookblog.blogspot.com/2013/05/falling-up-by-shel-silverstein.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabbit Ears Book Blog</a></b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1888385206740052084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1108922671" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1108922671" />
    <a title="Jenna Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35386315-jenna-kennedy"><img alt="Jenna Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411790391p2/35386315.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1108922671?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenna Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenna Kennedy" href="/user/show/35386315-jenna-kennedy">Jenna Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1108922671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12492618420853543114">With black, sketched illustrations on cream colored pages, the words flow down the pages as they do off of the reader’s tongue. The lyrical type narration use rhyme and repetition to show the adventure of Pinocchio (on page 46). An illustration of the wooden toy boy sits on the bottom of the page, with his nose as long as one, two, three lies. About ten stanzas long, this tale is only a part of the 171 page long book of poems for young readers. The silly and quirky stories use different types of</span>
  <span id="freeText12492618420853543114" style="display:none">With black, sketched illustrations on cream colored pages, the words flow down the pages as they do off of the reader’s tongue. The lyrical type narration use rhyme and repetition to show the adventure of Pinocchio (on page 46). An illustration of the wooden toy boy sits on the bottom of the page, with his nose as long as one, two, three lies. About ten stanzas long, this tale is only a part of the 171 page long book of poems for young readers. The silly and quirky stories use different types of poetic structures to show different themes- from deep messages about telling the truth to respecting grownups. The real life type themes are twisted with a mix of humor, these aspects combined appealing to kids who can relate to the messages. The lack of color and detailed illustration is made up by the witty and unique use of words. The words alone paint a picture in the readers mind, and evoke the children reader’s creativity and help to grow their analytical skills. As they read, the children can pick up on the poetic style and may feel inspired to write their own poems. Kudos to Shel Silverstein, the author of Falling Up, for giving children an uplifting and relatable inspiration to become a poet themselves.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12492618420853543114" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1196836092732533069"><b>One Word Review Game/Challenge</b>: Poems, poems, and even more poems<br/><br/><b>My Review</b>: I love all of Silverstein's poems, but this book has to be my favorite collection of his poems. I just found them very enjoyable to read, some made me crack a smile and a little laugh at times. This was a very fun book for me to read. I appreciate the way that Silverstein approaches the poems and crafts them together. Another thing I appreciated was how these poems aren't too advanced, at all, and they are something that</span>
  <span id="freeText1196836092732533069" style="display:none"><b>One Word Review Game/Challenge</b>: Poems, poems, and even more poems<br /><br /><b>My Review</b>: I love all of Silverstein's poems, but this book has to be my favorite collection of his poems. I just found them very enjoyable to read, some made me crack a smile and a little laugh at times. This was a very fun book for me to read. I appreciate the way that Silverstein approaches the poems and crafts them together. Another thing I appreciated was how these poems aren't too advanced, at all, and they are something that a younger student/child could read, or be read, and understand most of. The illustrations throughout are also cute. I love the hand-drawn look of them. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13338298837735019766">I received <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30119.Where_the_Sidewalk_Ends' title='Where the Sidewalk Ends by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>Where the Sidewalk Ends</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30118.A_Light_in_the_Attic' title='A Light in the Attic by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Light in the Attic</a> as presents as a child and they are still treasured possessions. We've read them together and our girls love the poems, especially our youngest. So for her birthday this year, I bought her this book. I think I read it years ago, but since I didn't own it, I don't know the poems nearly as well. <br/><br/>Our youngest only 'allows' us to read a couple of poems together each night, so it took us quite a long time to finish this book. It was just as </span>
  <span id="freeText13338298837735019766" style="display:none">I received <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30119.Where_the_Sidewalk_Ends" title="Where the Sidewalk Ends by Shel Silverstein" rel="nofollow noopener">Where the Sidewalk Ends</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30118.A_Light_in_the_Attic" title="A Light in the Attic by Shel Silverstein" rel="nofollow noopener">A Light in the Attic</a> as presents as a child and they are still treasured possessions. We've read them together and our girls love the poems, especially our youngest. So for her birthday this year, I bought her this book. I think I read it years ago, but since I didn't own it, I don't know the poems nearly as well. <br /><br />Our youngest only 'allows' us to read a couple of poems together each night, so it took us quite a long time to finish this book. It was just as enjoyable as the other books and we all looked forward to reading a couple of poems each night.</span>

<div id="review_98647747" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/98647747" />
    <a title="Alyssa Davila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3563011-alyssa-davila"><img alt="Alyssa Davila" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/98647747?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa Davila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa Davila" href="/user/show/3563011-alyssa-davila">Alyssa Davila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer98647747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15062647122992944109">i remember when i was in first grade, i had to do read a poem from his poem book <i>Falling Up</i> and i decided to pick a poem about this little kid going home and he notices a hat following him, the little kid gets all paranoid and relizes the hat has a tail. the little boy picks up the hat a comes to find that under the hat was either a little cat or a dog, i really cant remember, it was kind of a long time ago. but those poems made up my childhood. they made me think, analize, and got me to believe</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2017233408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11543533837667101701">This is an amusing if not quite classic set of poems for children. Some are fairly conventional offering relatively common and unexceptionable didacticism, but others definitely play into children's appreciation for the macabre, the cheeky, and the transgressive. There's rather more death and dismemberment than you might expect in work aimed at fairly young readers, but Silverstein knows that kids love to be repelled, grossed out, and scared, within certain limits, and he does not shy away from </span>
  <span id="freeText11543533837667101701" style="display:none">This is an amusing if not quite classic set of poems for children. Some are fairly conventional offering relatively common and unexceptionable didacticism, but others definitely play into children's appreciation for the macabre, the cheeky, and the transgressive. There's rather more death and dismemberment than you might expect in work aimed at fairly young readers, but Silverstein knows that kids love to be repelled, grossed out, and scared, within certain limits, and he does not shy away from appealing to kids' interest in the darker side. The whole thing is aided immeasurably by Silverstein's vivid, clearly-etched illustrations.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11543533837667101701" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16513719823933038114">Mostly word-play, rhymes, and puns. Each poem gets a drawing. It's all wacky, wild, fun, yet gruesome at times. Silverstein is obviously skilled, but this is not my favorite kind of poetry.<br/><br/>I still want to read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30119.Where_the_Sidewalk_Ends' title='Where the Sidewalk Ends by Shel Silverstein' rel='nofollow noopener'>Where the Sidewalk Ends</a>.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zxBrcphEa4oPXv0BpnEfr+7hd1xc4nH8l7R/0BN3U18+EsurH41NUYb/2wc1SZ9lQgNmJnXu9eAkgr1O9LfsDA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
